{
  "file_path": "/Users/sonmingi/.openclaw/workspace/issue-pilot/.repos/order-management-system/backend/api/src/main/kotlin/com/oms/api/config/VirtualThreadsConfig.kt",
  "content": "package com.oms.api.config\n\nimport org.springframework.context.annotation.Bean\nimport org.springframework.context.annotation.Configuration\nimport org.springframework.core.task.AsyncTaskExecutor\nimport org.springframework.core.task.support.TaskExecutorAdapter\nimport org.springframework.scheduling.annotation.EnableAsync\nimport java.util.concurrent.Executors\n\n/**\n * Virtual Threads configuration for Spring Boot 3.2+\n *\n * This configuration enables JDK 21 Virtual Threads for async operations,\n * providing lightweight concurrency for high-throughput applications.\n *\n * Virtual threads are suitable for I/O-bound operations and can scale to\n * millions of concurrent tasks without the overhead of traditional platform threads.\n */\n@Configuration\n@EnableAsync\nclass VirtualThreadsConfig {\n\n    /**\n     * Configures the default async task executor to use virtual threads.\n     *\n     * This executor will be used for:\n     * - @Async annotated methods\n     * - CompletableFuture async operations\n     * - Spring's async processing\n     *\n     * @return AsyncTaskExecutor backed by virtual threads\n     */\n    @Bean(name = [\"taskExecutor\", \"applicationTaskExecutor\"])\n    fun asyncTaskExecutor(): AsyncTaskExecutor {\n        return TaskExecutorAdapter(Executors.newVirtualThreadPerTaskExecutor())\n    }\n}\n"
}

'@/shared/components/ErrorBoundary'\"),\n    (r\"from ['\\\"]\\.\\.\\/\\.\\.\\/components\\/ErrorBoundary['\\\"]\", \"from '@/shared/components/ErrorBoundary'\"),\n]\n\ndef update_file_imports(file_path):\n    \"\"\"Update imports in a single file.\"\"\"\n    try:\n        with open(file_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:\n            content = f.read()\n\n        original_content = content\n\n        # Apply all replacement patterns\n        for pattern, replacement in IMPORT_REPLACEMENTS:\n            content = re.sub(pattern, replacement, content)\n\n        # Only write if content changed\n        if content != original_content:\n            with open(file_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:\n                f.write(content)\n            return True\n        return False\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\"Error updating {file_path}: {e}\")\n        return False\n\ndef main():\n    \"\"\"Main function to update all TypeScript files.\"\"\"\n    updated_count = 0\n    total_count = 0\n\n    # Walk through all .ts and .tsx files\n    for root, dirs, files in os.walk(BASE_DIR):\n        for file in files:\n            if file.endswith(('.ts', '.tsx')):\n                file_path = Path(root) / file\n                total_count += 1\n                if update_file_imports(file_path):\n                    updated_count += 1\n                    print(f\"Updated: {file_path.relative_to(BASE_DIR)}\")\n\n    print(f\"\\nSummary: Updated {updated_count} out of {total_count} files\")\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    main()\n"
}
```

## [2026-03-07T07:49:13.822Z] TOOL_USE

Using tool: Write

### Tool: `Write`

```json
{
  "file_path": "/Users/sonmingi/.openclaw/workspace/issue-pilot/.repos/order-management-system/frontend/fix_component_imports.py",
  "content": "#!/usr/bin/env python3\n\"\"\"\nFix intra-feature component imports after restructuring.\n\"\"\"\nimport os\nimport re\nfrom pathlib import Path\n\nBASE_DIR = Path(__file__).parent / \"src\"\n\ndef fix_component_imports(file_path):\n    \"\"\"Fix imports from ../components/ to ./ for files already in components folder.\"\"\"\n    try:\n        with open(file_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:\n            content = f.read()\n\n        original_content = content\n\n        # Check if file is in a components directory\n        if '/components/' in str(file_path):\n            # Replace ../components/ with ./\n            content = re.sub(r\"from ['\\\"]\\.\\.\\/components\\/\", \"from './\", content)\n            # Replace ../../components/ with @/shared/components/ (shared components)\n            content = re.sub(r\"from ['\\\"]\\.\\.\\/\\.\\.\\/\\.\\.\\/components\\/\", \"from '@/shared/components/\", content)\n\n        # Only write if content changed\n        if content != original_content:\n            with open(file_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:\n                f.write(content)\n            return True\n        return False\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\"Error updating {file_path}: {e}\")\n        return False\n\ndef main():\n    \"\"\"Main function.\"\"\"\n    updated_count = 0\n    total_count = 0\n\n    for root, dirs, files in os.walk(BASE_DIR):\n        for file in files:\n            if file.endswith(('.ts', '.tsx')):\n                file_path = Path(root) / file\n                total_count += 1\n                if fix_component_imports(file_path):\n                    updated_count += 1\n                    print(f\"Updated: {file_path.relative_to(BASE_DIR)}\")\n\n    print(f\"\\nSummary: Updated {updated_count} out of {total_count} files\")\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    main()\n"
}
```

  "content": "import { QueryClient } from '@tanstack/react-query';\n\n/**\n * Configured QueryClient instance for React Query\n *\n * Default options:\n * - staleTime: 5 minutes - data considered fresh for 5 mins\n * - cacheTime: 10 minutes - unused data kept in cache for 10 mins\n * - retry: 1 - failed queries retry once before erroring\n * - refetchOnWindowFocus: false - don't auto-refetch on window focus\n */\nexport const queryClient = new QueryClient({\n  defaultOptions: {\n    queries: {\n      staleTime: 5 * 60 * 1000, // 5 minutes\n      gcTime: 10 * 60 * 1000, // 10 minutes (formerly cacheTime)\n      retry: 1,\n      refetchOnWindowFocus: false,\n    },\n    mutations: {\n      retry: 0,\n    },\n  },\n});\n\n/**\n * Query keys for consistent cache key management\n *\n * Usage:\n * - queryKeys.orders.all - ['orders']\n * - queryKeys.orders.detail(id) - ['orders', id]\n * - queryKeys.inventory.all - ['inventory']\n */\nexport const queryKeys = {\n  orders: {\n    all: ['orders'] as const,\n    detail: (id: string) => ['orders', id] as const,\n  },\n  inventory: {\n    all: ['inventory'] as const,\n    detail: (id: string) => ['inventory', id] as const,\n  },\n  products: {\n    all: ['products'] as const,\n    detail: (id: string) => ['products', id] as const,\n  },\n  shipping: {\n    all: ['shipping'] as const,\n    detail: (id: string) => ['shipping', id] as const,\n  },\n  claims: {\n    all: ['claims'] as const,\n    detail: (id: string) => ['claims', id] as const,\n  },\n};\n"
}
```

## [2026-03-07T07:54:28.002Z] TOOL_USE

Using tool: Write

### Tool: `Write`

```json
{
  "file_path": "/Users/sonmingi/.openclaw/workspace/issue-pilot/.repos/order-management-system/frontend/src/features/orders/hooks/useOrderQueries.ts",
  "content": "import { useQuery, useMutation, useQueryClient } from '@tanstack/react-query';\nimport api from '@/core/api/api';\nimport { queryKeys } from '@/core/api/queryClient';\nimport { Order } from '@/shared/types/types';\n\n/**\n * Fetch all orders from the API\n */\nconst fetchOrders = async (): Promise<Order[]> => {\n  const response = await api.get<Order[]>('/orders');\n  return response.data;\n};\n\n/**\n * Fetch a single order by ID\n */\nconst fetchOrder = async (id: string): Promise<Order> => {\n  const response = await api.get<Order>(`/orders/${id}`);\n  return response.data;\n};\n\n/**\n * Create a new order\n */\nconst createOrder = async (orderData: Partial<Order>): Promise<Order> => {\n  const response = await api.post<Order>('/orders', orderData);\n  return response.data;\n};\n\n/**\n * Update an existing order\n */\nconst updateOrder = async ({ id, data }: { id: string; data: Partial<Order> }): Promise<Order> => {\n  const response = await api.put<Order>(`/orders/${id}`, data);\n  return response.data;\n};\n\n/**\n * Hook to fetch all orders\n *\n * @returns Query result with orders data, loading, and error states\n */\nexport const useOrders = () => {\n  return useQuery({\n    queryKey: queryKeys.orders.all,\n    queryFn: fetchOrders,\n  });\n};\n\n/**\n * Hook to fetch a single order by ID\n *\n * @param id - Order ID\n * @param enabled - Whether the query should run (default: true when id exists)\n * @returns Query result with order data, loading, and error states\n */\nexport const useOrder = (id: string | null, enabled = true) => {\n  return useQuery({\n    queryKey: queryKeys.orders.detail(id || ''),\n    queryFn: () => fetchOrder(id!),\n    enabled: enabled && !!id,\n  });\n};\n\n/**\n * Hook to create a new order\n *\n * @returns Mutation object with mutate function and status\n */\nexport const useCreateOrder = () => {\n  const queryClient = useQueryClient();\n\n  return useMutation({\n    mutationFn: createOrder,\n    onSuccess: () => {\n      // Invalidate orders list to refetch after creation\n      queryClient.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: queryKeys.orders.all });\n    },\n  });\n};\n\n/**\n * Hook to update an existing order\n *\n * @returns Mutation object with mutate function and status\n */\nexport const useUpdateOrder = () => {\n  const queryClient = useQueryClient();\n\n  return useMutation({\n    mutationFn: updateOrder,\n    onSuccess: (data) => {\n      // Invalidate both the list and the specific order\n      queryClient.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: queryKeys.orders.all });\n      queryClient.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: queryKeys.orders.detail(data.id) });\n    },\n  });\n};\n"
}
```

## [2026-03-07T07:54:53.219Z] TOOL_USE

Using tool: Write

### Tool: `Write`

```json
{
  "file_path": "/Users/sonmingi/.openclaw/workspace/issue-pilot/.repos/order-management-system/frontend/src/features/inventory/hooks/useInventoryQueries.ts",
  "content": "import { useQuery, useMutation, useQueryClient } from '@tanstack/react-query';\nimport api from '@/core/api/api';\nimport { queryKeys } from '@/core/api/queryClient';\nimport { Inventory } from '@/shared/types/types';\n\n/**\n * Fetch all inventory items from the API\n */\nconst fetchInventory = async (): Promise<Inventory[]> => {\n  const response = await api.get<Inventory[]>('/inventory');\n  return response.data;\n};\n\n/**\n * Fetch a single inventory item by ID\n */\nconst fetchInventoryItem = async (id: string): Promise<Inventory> => {\n  const response = await api.get<Inventory>(`/inventory/${id}`);\n  return response.data;\n};\n\n/**\n * Adjust stock for an inventory item\n */\ninterface StockAdjustment {\n  productId: string;\n  warehouse: string;\n  quantity: number;\n  reason: string;\n  type: 'increase' | 'decrease';\n}\n\nconst adjustStock = async (adjustment: StockAdjustment): Promise<Inventory> => {\n  const response = await api.post<Inventory>('/inventory/adjust', adjustment);\n  return response.data;\n};\n\n/**\n * Hook to fetch all inventory items\n *\n * @returns Query result with inventory data, loading, and error states\n */\nexport const useInventory = () => {\n  return useQuery({\n    queryKey: queryKeys.inventory.all,\n    queryFn: fetchInventory,\n  });\n};\n\n/**\n * Hook to fetch a single inventory item by ID\n *\n * @param id - Inventory item ID (product ID)\n * @param enabled - Whether the query should run (default: true when id exists)\n * @returns Query result with inventory item data, loading, and error states\n */\nexport const useInventoryItem = (id: string | null, enabled = true) => {\n  return useQuery({\n    queryKey: queryKeys.inventory.detail(id || ''),\n    queryFn: () => fetchInventoryItem(id!),\n    enabled: enabled && !!id,\n  });\n};\n\n/**\n * Hook to adjust stock for an inventory item\n *\n * @returns Mutation object with mutate function and status\n */\nexport const useAdjustStock = () => {\n  const queryClient = useQueryClient();\n\n  return useMutation({\n    mutationFn: adjustStock,\n    onSuccess: (data) => {\n      // Invalidate inventory list to refetch after adjustment\n      queryClient.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: queryKeys.inventory.all });\n      // Invalidate the specific inventory item\n      queryClient.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: queryKeys.inventory.detail(data.productId) });\n    },\n  });\n};\n"
}
```

{
  "file_path": "/Users/sonmingi/.openclaw/workspace/issue-pilot/.repos/order-management-system/.github/workflows/docker-publish.yml",
  "content": "name: Docker Publish\n\non:\n  push:\n    tags:\n      - 'v*.*.*'\n    branches:\n      - main\n  workflow_dispatch:\n    inputs:\n      tag:\n        description: 'Image tag (e.g., v1.0.0, latest)'\n        required: false\n        default: 'latest'\n\nenv:\n  REGISTRY: ghcr.io\n  IMAGE_NAME: ${{ github.repository }}\n\njobs:\n  build-and-push-backend:\n    name: Build and Push Backend Image\n    runs-on: ubuntu-latest\n    permissions:\n      contents: read\n      packages: write\n\n    steps:\n      - name: Checkout code\n        uses: actions/checkout@v4\n\n      - name: Set up Docker Buildx\n        uses: docker/setup-buildx-action@v3\n\n      - name: Log in to GitHub Container Registry\n        uses: docker/login-action@v3\n        with:\n          registry: ${{ env.REGISTRY }}\n          username: ${{ github.actor }}\n          password: ${{ secrets.GITHUB_TOKEN }}\n\n      - name: Extract metadata for Docker\n        id: meta\n        uses: docker/metadata-action@v5\n        with:\n          images: ${{ env.REGISTRY }}/${{ env.IMAGE_NAME }}-backend\n          tags: |\n            type=ref,event=branch\n            type=ref,event=pr\n            type=semver,pattern={{version}}\n            type=semver,pattern={{major}}.{{minor}}\n            type=semver,pattern={{major}}\n            type=raw,value=latest,enable={{is_default_branch}}\n            type=raw,value=${{ github.event.inputs.tag }},enable=${{ github.event_name == 'workflow_dispatch' }}\n\n      - name: Build and push Backend image\n        uses: docker/build-push-action@v6\n        with:\n          context: ./backend\n          file: ./backend/Dockerfile\n          platforms: linux/amd64,linux/arm64\n          push: true\n          tags: ${{ steps.meta.outputs.tags }}\n          labels: ${{ steps.meta.outputs.labels }}\n          cache-from: type=gha\n          cache-to: type=gha,mode=max\n          build-args: |\n            VERSION=${{ github.ref_name }}\n            COMMIT_SHA=${{ github.sha }}\n\n  build-and-push-frontend:\n    name: Build and Push Frontend Image\n    runs-on: ubuntu-latest\n    permissions:\n      contents: read\n      packages: write\n\n    steps:\n      - name: Checkout code\n        uses: actions/checkout@v4\n\n      - name: Set up Docker Buildx\n        uses: docker/setup-buildx-action@v3\n\n      - name: Log in to GitHub Container Registry\n        uses: docker/login-action@v3\n        with:\n          registry: ${{ env.REGISTRY }}\n          username: ${{ github.actor }}\n          password: ${{ secrets.GITHUB_TOKEN }}\n\n      - name: Extract metadata for Docker\n        id: meta\n        uses: docker/metadata-action@v5\n        with:\n          images: ${{ env.REGISTRY }}/${{ env.IMAGE_NAME }}-frontend\n          tags: |\n            type=ref,event=branch\n            type=ref,event=pr\n            type=semver,pattern={{version}}\n            type=semver,pattern={{major}}.{{minor}}\n            type=semver,pattern={{major}}\n            type=raw,value=latest,enable={{is_default_branch}}\n            type=raw,value=${{ github.event.inputs.tag }},enable=${{ github.event_name == 'workflow_dispatch' }}\n\n      - name: Build and push Frontend image\n        uses: docker/build-push-action@v6\n        with:\n          context: ./frontend\n          file: ./frontend/Dockerfile\n          platforms: linux/amd64,linux/arm64\n          push: true\n          tags: ${{ steps.meta.outputs.tags }}\n          labels: ${{ steps.meta.outputs.labels }}\n          cache-from: type=gha\n          cache-to: type=gha,mode=max\n          build-args: |\n            VERSION=${{ github.ref_name }}\n            COMMIT_SHA=${{ github.sha }}\n\n  verify-images:\n    name: Verify Published Images\n    runs-on: ubuntu-latest\n    needs: [build-and-push-backend, build-and-push-frontend]\n\n    steps:\n      - name: Verify backend image\n        run: |\n          docker pull ${{ env.REGISTRY }}/${{ env.IMAGE_NAME }}-backend:latest\n          docker inspect ${{ env.REGISTRY }}/${{ env.IMAGE_NAME }}-backend:latest\n\n      - name: Verify frontend image\n        run: |\n          docker pull ${{ env.REGISTRY }}/${{ env.IMAGE_NAME }}-frontend:latest\n          docker inspect ${{ env.REGISTRY }}/${{ env.IMAGE_NAME }}-frontend:latest\n\n      - name: Summary\n        run: |\n          echo \"### Docker Images Published Successfully! :rocket:\" >> $GITHUB_STEP_SUMMARY\n          echo \"\" >> $GITHUB_STEP_SUMMARY\n          echo \"Backend Image: \\`${{ env.REGISTRY }}/${{ env.IMAGE_NAME }}-backend:latest\\`\" >> $GITHUB_STEP_SUMMARY\n          echo \"Frontend Image: \\`${{ env.REGISTRY }}/${{ env.IMAGE_NAME }}-frontend:latest\\`\" >> $GITHUB_STEP_SUMMARY\n"
}

## [2026-03-07T08:02:18.819Z] TOOL_USE

Using tool: Write

### Tool: `Write`

```json
{
  "file_path": "/Users/sonmingi/.openclaw/workspace/issue-pilot/.repos/order-management-system/ARCHITECTURE.md",
  "content": "# Global OMS - System Architecture\n\n## Overview\n\nGlobal OMS is an enterprise-grade order management system built using Domain-Driven Design (DDD) principles and event-driven architecture. The system is designed to handle complex e-commerce operations at scale with support for multi-channel sales, global inventory management, and automated order processing.\n\n## Architecture Principles\n\n- **Domain-Driven Design (DDD)**: Business logic organized into bounded contexts\n- **Event-Driven Architecture**: Asynchronous communication between contexts\n- **Hexagonal Architecture**: Clean separation of business logic from infrastructure\n- **Microservices Ready**: Modular design allows for future service extraction\n- **API-First**: RESTful APIs with OpenAPI/Swagger documentation\n\n## System Architecture\n\n```\n┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n│                          Frontend (React 19)                    │\n│  ┌──────────────┐  ┌──────────────┐  ┌──────────────┐          │\n│  │   Features   │  │ React Query  │  │   Zustand    │          │\n│  │   (Pages)    │  │ (Server)     │  │    (UI)      │          │\n│  └──────────────┘  └──────────────┘  └──────────────┘          │\n└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n                              ▼\n┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n│                     API Layer (Spring Boot 3.2)                 │\n│  ┌──────────────┐  ┌──────────────┐  ┌──────────────┐          │\n│  │ REST         │  │ WebSocket    │  │   GraphQL    │          │\n│  │ Controllers  │  │ (Future)     │  │  (Future)    │          │\n│  └──────────────┘  └──────────────┘  └──────────────┘          │\n└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n                              ▼\n┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n│                   Application Layer (Use Cases)                 │\n│  ┌──────────────┐  ┌──────────────┐  ┌──────────────┐          │\n│  │  Application │  │    Event     │  │  Integration │          │\n│  │   Services   │  │   Handlers   │  │   Services   │          │\n│  └──────────────┘  └──────────────┘  └──────────────┘          │\n└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n                              ▼\n┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n│              Domain Layer (Bounded Contexts)                    │\n│  ┌──────────────┐  ┌──────────────┐  ┌──────────────┐          │\n│  │    Order     │  │   Channel    │  │  Inventory   │          │\n│  │   Context    │  │   Context    │  │   Context    │          │\n│  └──────────────┘  └──────────────┘  └──────────────┘          │\n│  ┌──────────────┐  ┌──────────────┐  ┌──────────────┐          │\n│  │    Claim     │  │  Settlement  │  │  Automation  │          │\n│  │   Context    │  │   Context    │  │   Context    │          │\n│  └──────────────┘  └──────────────┘  └──────────────┘          │\n│  ┌──────────────┐  ┌──────────────┐  ┌──────────────┐          │\n│  │   Strategy   │  │   Catalog    │  │   Identity   │          │\n│  │   Context    │  │   Context    │  │   Context    │          │\n│  └──────────────┘  └──────────────┘  └──────────────┘          │\n└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n                              ▼\n┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n│                 Infrastructure Layer                            │\n│  ┌──────────────┐  ┌──────────────┐  ┌──────────────┐          │\n│  │  PostgreSQL  │  │   MongoDB    │  │    Redis     │          │\n│  │   (RDBMS)    │  │  (Documents) │  │   (Cache)    │          │\n│  └──────────────┘  └──────────────┘  └──────────────┘          │\n└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n```\n\n## Backend Architecture\n\n### Technology Stack\n\n- **JDK 21**: Latest LTS with Virtual Threads for improved concurrency\n- **Kotlin 1.9**: Modern JVM language with concise syntax\n- **Spring Boot 3.2**: Application framework\n- **PostgreSQL 16**: Primary relational database\n- **MongoDB 7.0**: Document store for flexible schemas\n- **Redis 7**: Caching and session management\n\n### Bounded Contexts (DDD Modules)\n\n#### 1. Order Context (`domain-order`)\n- Manages order lifecycle\n- Order placement, modification, cancellation\n- Order status tracking\n- Order splitting and merging\n\n#### 2. Channel Context (`domain-channel`)\n- Multi-channel integration (marketplaces, own stores)\n- Channel-specific policies and fees\n- Warehouse and fulfillment center management\n- Channel performance monitoring\n\n#### 3. Inventory Context (`domain-inventory`)\n- Real-time inventory synchronization\n- Multi-warehouse inventory allocation\n- Safety stock alerts\n- Inventory history tracking\n\n#### 4. Claim Context (`domain-claim`)\n- Return, exchange, refund processing\n- Claim workflow management\n- Customer compensation policies\n- Claim statistics and analytics\n\n#### 5. Settlement Context (`domain-settlement`)\n- Channel-specific settlement automation\n- Fee calculation and management\n- Settlement report generation\n- Settlement history and queries\n\n#### 6. Automation Context (`domain-automation`)\n- Rule-based automated processing\n- Conditional action triggers\n- Workflow automation\n\n#### 7. Strategy Context (`domain-strategy`)\n- Inventory allocation strategies\n- Global operations readiness\n- Strategic decision support\n\n#### 8. Catalog Context (`domain-catalog`)\n- Product information management\n- SKU management\n- Product categorization\n\n#### 9. Identity Context (`domain-identity`)\n- Company/organization management\n- User authentication and authorization\n- Role-based access control (RBAC)\n- Multi-tenancy support\n\n### Module Structure\n\n```\nbackend/\n├── api/                        # REST API layer\n├── application/                # Application services (use cases)\n├── domain/\n│   ├── domain-order/          # Order bounded context\n│   ├── domain-channel/        # Channel bounded context\n│   ├── domain-inventory/      # Inventory bounded context\n│   ├── domain-claim/          # Claim bounded context\n│   ├── domain-settlement/     # Settlement bounded context\n│   ├── domain-automation/     # Automation bounded context\n│   ├── domain-strategy/       # Strategy bounded context\n│   ├── domain-catalog/        # Catalog bounded context\n│   └── domain-identity/       # Identity bounded context\n├── infrastructure/\n│   ├── infra-postgres/        # JPA repositories (PostgreSQL)\n│   ├── infra-mongo/           # MongoDB repositories\n│   └── infra-redis/           # Redis cache\n└── core/\n    └── core-domain/           # Shared domain (base entities, events)\n```\n\n### JDK 21 Virtual Threads\n\nThe backend leverages JDK 21's Virtual Threads for improved concurrency:\n\n- **Spring MVC**: Configured to use virtual threads for request handling\n- **Async Operations**: Database queries and API calls benefit from lightweight threads\n- **Scalability**: Handle thousands of concurrent connections with minimal resource overhead\n\nConfiguration in `application.yml`:\n```yaml\nspring:\n  threads:\n    virtual:\n      enabled: true\n```\n\n### Database Strategy\n\n- **PostgreSQL**: Transactional data (orders, inventory, settlements)\n- **MongoDB**: Flexible schemas (events, logs, analytics)\n- **Redis**: Session state, caching, real-time data\n\n## Frontend Architecture\n\n### Technology Stack\n\n- **React 19**: Modern UI library with server components (future)\n- **TypeScript**: Type-safe JavaScript\n- **Vite 6**: Fast build tool and dev server\n- **pnpm**: Efficient package management\n- **React Query**: Server state management\n- **Zustand**: UI state management\n- **i18next**: Internationalization\n\n### State Management Strategy\n\n#### React Query (Server State)\n- API data fetching and caching\n- Automatic background refetching\n- Optimistic updates\n- Request deduplication\n\n#### Zustand (UI State)\n- Local UI state (modals, forms, selections)\n- Theme preferences\n- User session state\n\n**Separation Rationale**: Clear boundary between server-synchronized data (React Query) and local UI concerns (Zustand).\n\n### Feature-Based Architecture\n\n```\nfrontend/src/\n├── features/\n│   ├── orders/\n│   │   ├── components/        # Order-specific components\n│   │   ├── hooks/             # Order-related hooks\n│   │   ├── api/               # Order API calls (React Query)\n│   │   └── store/             # Order UI state (Zustand)\n│   ├── inventory/\n│   ├── channels/\n│   └── ...\n├── components/\n│   └── ui/                    # Shared UI components\n├── lib/\n│   ├── api/                   # API client setup\n│   ├── query/                 # React Query config\n│   └── i18n/                  # i18n setup\n└── App.tsx\n```\n\n### Component Patterns\n\n- **Atomic Design**: Atoms → Molecules → Organisms → Templates → Pages\n- **Compound Components**: Complex components with flexible composition\n- **Render Props & Hooks**: Reusable logic extraction\n\n## Infrastructure\n\n### Docker Compose Setup\n\nTwo deployment modes:\n\n1. **Full Stack** (`docker-compose.yml`):\n   - Backend (Spring Boot)\n   - Frontend (Vite + React)\n   - PostgreSQL\n   - MongoDB\n   - Redis\n\n2. **Infrastructure Only** (`docker-compose.dev.yml`):\n   - PostgreSQL (with Adminer)\n   - MongoDB (with Mongo Express)\n   - Redis\n   - For local development of backend/frontend\n\n### Database Initialization\n\n- **PostgreSQL**: Schema initialization scripts in `docker/postgres/init/`\n- **MongoDB**: Collections and indexes created on first run\n- **Redis**: No initialization required\n\n## CI/CD Pipeline\n\n### GitHub Actions Workflows\n\n#### Backend CI (`.github/workflows/backend-ci.yml`)\n- Triggered on push/PR to `main` affecting `backend/**`\n- Steps:\n  1. Setup JDK 21\n  2. Cache Gradle dependencies\n  3. Run `./gradlew build` (compile + test)\n  4. Run code quality checks (detekt, ktlint)\n\n#### Frontend CI (`.github/workflows/frontend-ci.yml`)\n- Triggered on push/PR to `main` affecting `frontend/**`\n- Steps:\n  1. Setup Node.js and pnpm\n  2. Cache pnpm dependencies\n  3. Run `pnpm install`\n  4. Run `pnpm type-check` (TypeScript)\n  5. Run `pnpm lint` (ESLint)\n  6. Run `pnpm test` (Vitest)\n  7. Run `pnpm build` (production build)\n\n#### Docker Build (`.github/workflows/docker-build.yml`)\n- Triggered on push/PR to `main` affecting Docker files\n- Validates Docker Compose builds\n\n### Future CI/CD Enhancements\n- Automated deployments to staging/production\n- Database migration checks\n- E2E testing with Playwright\n- Performance benchmarking\n- Security scanning (Snyk, Trivy)\n\n## Code Quality\n\n### Backend\n- **detekt**: Static code analysis for Kotlin\n- **ktlint**: Kotlin code style enforcement\n- Configuration: `detekt.yml`, `.editorconfig`\n\n### Frontend\n- **ESLint 9**: Linting with flat config system\n- **Prettier**: Code formatting\n- **TypeScript**: Type checking with strict mode\n- Configuration: `eslint.config.js`, `.prettierrc`, `tsconfig.json`\n\n## Testing Strategy\n\n### Backend Testing (Planned)\n- **Unit Tests**: JUnit 5, MockK for mocking\n- **Integration Tests**: Testcontainers for database tests\n- **Architecture Tests**: ArchUnit for enforcing architectural rules\n- **API Tests**: Spring REST Docs\n\n### Frontend Testing\n- **Unit Tests**: Vitest for component logic\n- **Component Tests**: Testing Library for React components\n- **E2E Tests** (Planned): Playwright for user flows\n- **Visual Regression** (Planned): Percy or Chromatic\n\n### Test Coverage Goals\n- Backend: >80% line coverage\n- Frontend: >70% line coverage\n- Critical paths: 100% coverage\n\n## Security Considerations\n\n### Authentication & Authorization\n- JWT-based authentication\n- Role-based access control (RBAC)\n- Multi-tenancy isolation\n\n### Data Protection\n- Encrypted passwords (bcrypt)\n- HTTPS enforcement in production\n- Environment variable secrets management\n\n### API Security\n- Rate limiting\n- CORS configuration\n- Input validation and sanitization\n- SQL injection prevention (JPA/Hibernate)\n\n## Scalability & Performance\n\n### Backend\n- **Virtual Threads**: Lightweight concurrency (JDK 21)\n- **Connection Pooling**: HikariCP for database connections\n- **Caching**: Redis for frequently accessed data\n- **Async Processing**: Event-driven architecture for background tasks\n\n### Frontend\n- **Code Splitting**: Route-based lazy loading\n- **React Query Caching**: Reduce API calls\n- **Optimistic Updates**: Instant UI feedback\n- **Vite**: Fast HMR and optimized builds\n\n### Database\n- **Indexing**: Optimized queries with proper indexes\n- **Read Replicas** (Future): Scale read operations\n- **Sharding** (Future): Horizontal scaling for PostgreSQL\n\n## Monitoring & Observability (Planned)\n\n- **Application Metrics**: Spring Boot Actuator + Micrometer\n- **Logging**: Structured logging with Logback\n- **Tracing**: Distributed tracing with OpenTelemetry\n- **APM**: Application Performance Monitoring (e.g., New Relic, Datadog)\n- **Error Tracking**: Sentry for frontend/backend errors\n\n## Future Enhancements\n\n### Architecture Evolution\n- **Event Sourcing**: Audit trail for critical operations\n- **CQRS**: Separate read/write models for complex queries\n- **Microservices**: Extract bounded contexts into separate services\n- **GraphQL**: Flexible API queries for frontend\n\n### Technology Additions\n- **Kafka**: Event streaming for inter-service communication\n- **Elasticsearch**: Full-text search and analytics\n- **gRPC**: High-performance inter-service communication\n- **Kubernetes**: Container orchestration for production\n\n## References\n\n- [Domain-Driven Design (DDD)](https://martinfowler.com/bliki/DomainDrivenDesign.html)\n- [Hexagonal Architecture](https://alistair.cockburn.us/hexagonal-architecture/)\n- [JDK 21 Virtual Threads](https://openjdk.org/jeps/444)\n- [React Query](https://tanstack.com/query/latest)\n- [Zustand](https://zustand-demo.pmnd.rs/)\n"
}
```

  "content": "# Contributing to Global OMS\n\nThank you for your interest in contributing to Global OMS! This document provides guidelines and instructions for contributing to the project.\n\n## Table of Contents\n\n- [Getting Started](#getting-started)\n- [Development Setup](#development-setup)\n- [Code Standards](#code-standards)\n- [Commit Guidelines](#commit-guidelines)\n- [Pull Request Process](#pull-request-process)\n- [Testing Requirements](#testing-requirements)\n- [Code Review Process](#code-review-process)\n\n## Getting Started\n\n### Prerequisites\n\nBefore you begin, ensure you have the following installed:\n\n- **JDK 21+**: Required for backend development\n- **pnpm 9+**: Package manager for frontend\n- **Docker Desktop 4.0+**: For running infrastructure services\n- **Git**: Version control\n\n### Fork and Clone\n\n1. Fork the repository on GitHub\n2. Clone your fork locally:\n   ```bash\n   git clone https://github.com/YOUR_USERNAME/order-management-system.git\n   cd order-management-system\n   ```\n3. Add upstream remote:\n   ```bash\n   git remote add upstream https://github.com/smk692/order-management-system.git\n   ```\n\n## Development Setup\n\n### Backend Setup\n\n1. Start infrastructure services:\n   ```bash\n   docker compose -f docker-compose.dev.yml up -d\n   ```\n\n2. Run the backend:\n   ```bash\n   cd backend\n   ./gradlew :api:bootRun\n   ```\n\n3. Access Swagger UI at http://localhost:8080/swagger-ui/\n\n### Frontend Setup\n\n1. Install dependencies:\n   ```bash\n   cd frontend\n   pnpm install\n   ```\n\n2. Run development server:\n   ```bash\n   pnpm dev\n   ```\n\n3. Access the app at http://localhost:3000\n\n### Verify Setup\n\n- Backend health check: `curl http://localhost:8080/actuator/health`\n- Frontend should open automatically in your browser\n\n## Code Standards\n\n### Backend (Kotlin)\n\n#### Style Guide\n\nFollow Kotlin coding conventions:\n- Use 4 spaces for indentation\n- Maximum line length: 120 characters\n- Use meaningful variable and function names\n- Prefer `val` over `var` when possible\n- Use data classes for DTOs\n\n#### Code Quality Tools\n\nRun before committing:\n```bash\n# Format code\n./gradlew ktlintFormat\n\n# Check style\n./gradlew ktlintCheck\n\n# Static analysis\n./gradlew detekt\n\n# All checks\n./gradlew ktlintCheck detekt test\n```\n\n#### Package Structure\n\n```\ndomain-{context}/\n├── model/              # Domain entities, value objects\n├── repository/         # Repository interfaces\n├── service/            # Domain services\n└── event/              # Domain events\n```\n\n#### Best Practices\n\n- Keep domain logic in domain modules\n- Use dependency injection (Spring)\n- Write self-documenting code\n- Add KDoc for public APIs\n- Follow SOLID principles\n- Use sealed classes for type hierarchies\n\n### Frontend (TypeScript/React)\n\n#### Style Guide\n\nFollow Airbnb React/TypeScript conventions:\n- Use 2 spaces for indentation\n- Maximum line length: 100 characters\n- Use functional components with hooks\n- Prefer named exports for components\n- Use TypeScript strict mode\n\n#### Code Quality Tools\n\nRun before committing:\n```bash\n# Format code\npnpm format\n\n# Check formatting\npnpm format:check\n\n# Lint\npnpm lint\n\n# Type check\npnpm type-check\n\n# All checks\npnpm lint && pnpm format:check && pnpm type-check && pnpm test\n```\n\n#### Component Structure\n\n```tsx\n// features/orders/components/OrderList.tsx\nimport { useState } from 'react';\nimport { useOrders } from '../hooks/useOrders';\n\nexport function OrderList() {\n  // Hooks first\n  const { data, isLoading } = useOrders();\n  const [selected, setSelected] = useState<string | null>(null);\n\n  // Early returns\n  if (isLoading) return <LoadingSpinner />;\n\n  // Main render\n  return (\n    <div>\n      {data?.map(order => (\n        <OrderItem key={order.id} order={order} />\n      ))}\n    </div>\n  );\n}\n```\n\n#### Best Practices\n\n- Use React Query for server state\n- Use Zustand for UI state\n- Avoid prop drilling (use context or state management)\n- Keep components small and focused\n- Use TypeScript for type safety\n- Write accessible HTML (ARIA attributes)\n\n## Commit Guidelines\n\n### Commit Message Format\n\nWe follow the [Conventional Commits](https://www.conventionalcommits.org/) specification:\n\n```\n<type>(<scope>): <subject>\n\n<body>\n\n<footer>\n```\n\n#### Types\n\n- `feat`: New feature\n- `fix`: Bug fix\n- `docs`: Documentation changes\n- `style`: Code style changes (formatting, no logic change)\n- `refactor`: Code refactoring (no feature or bug fix)\n- `perf`: Performance improvements\n- `test`: Adding or updating tests\n- `chore`: Build process, dependencies, tooling\n- `ci`: CI/CD configuration changes\n\n#### Scope\n\nSpecify the affected module or feature:\n- `order`: Order context\n- `inventory`: Inventory context\n- `channel`: Channel context\n- `claim`: Claim context\n- `settlement`: Settlement context\n- `automation`: Automation context\n- `strategy`: Strategy context\n- `catalog`: Catalog context\n- `identity`: Identity context\n- `api`: API layer\n- `frontend`: Frontend code\n- `infra`: Infrastructure code\n\n#### Examples\n\n```bash\n# Feature\nfeat(order): add order cancellation endpoint\n\n# Bug fix\nfix(inventory): correct stock calculation for split orders\n\n# Documentation\ndocs(readme): update setup instructions for PostgreSQL\n\n# Refactoring\nrefactor(claim): simplify claim status workflow\n\n# Multiple scopes\nfeat(order,inventory): add inventory reservation on order creation\n```\n\n### Commit Best Practices\n\n- Keep commits atomic (one logical change per commit)\n- Write clear, descriptive commit messages\n- Reference issue numbers: `feat(order): add search (#123)`\n- Use imperative mood: \"add\" not \"added\" or \"adds\"\n\n## Pull Request Process\n\n### Before Creating a PR\n\n1. **Update from upstream**:\n   ```bash\n   git fetch upstream\n   git rebase upstream/main\n   ```\n\n2. **Run all checks**:\n   ```bash\n   # Backend\n   cd backend\n   ./gradlew ktlintCheck detekt test\n\n   # Frontend\n   cd frontend\n   pnpm lint && pnpm format:check && pnpm type-check && pnpm test\n   ```\n\n3. **Verify build**:\n   ```bash\n   # Backend\n   ./gradlew build\n\n   # Frontend\n   pnpm build\n   ```\n\n### Creating a PR\n\n1. Push your branch:\n   ```bash\n   git push origin feature/your-feature-name\n   ```\n\n2. Open a PR on GitHub\n\n3. Fill out the PR template:\n   - **Title**: Use conventional commit format\n   - **Description**: Explain what and why\n   - **Related Issues**: Link to issue(s)\n   - **Screenshots**: For UI changes\n   - **Testing**: How you tested the changes\n\n### PR Template\n\n```markdown\n## Description\nBrief description of changes\n\n## Type of Change\n- [ ] Bug fix\n- [ ] New feature\n- [ ] Breaking change\n- [ ] Documentation update\n\n## Related Issues\nCloses #123\n\n## Changes Made\n- Change 1\n- Change 2\n\n## Testing\nHow the changes were tested\n\n## Screenshots (if applicable)\n\n## Checklist\n- [ ] Code follows project style guidelines\n- [ ] Self-review completed\n- [ ] Comments added for complex logic\n- [ ] Documentation updated\n- [ ] No new warnings\n- [ ] Tests added/updated\n- [ ] All tests pass\n- [ ] Build succeeds\n```\n\n### PR Review Criteria\n\nYour PR will be reviewed for:\n- **Functionality**: Does it work as intended?\n- **Code Quality**: Is it clean, readable, maintainable?\n- **Tests**: Are there adequate tests?\n- **Documentation**: Is documentation updated?\n- **Performance**: Are there performance concerns?\n- **Security**: Are there security implications?\n\n## Testing Requirements\n\n### Backend Testing\n\n#### Unit Tests\n\nWrite unit tests for:\n- Domain logic (entities, value objects)\n- Business rules and validations\n- Application services\n\nExample with JUnit 5 and MockK:\n```kotlin\n@Test\nfun `should create order when inventory is available`() {\n    // Given\n    val order = Order(...)\n    every { inventoryService.checkAvailability(...) } returns true\n\n    // When\n    val result = orderService.createOrder(order)\n\n    // Then\n    assertThat(result).isNotNull()\n    verify { inventoryService.reserveStock(...) }\n}\n```\n\n#### Integration Tests\n\nWrite integration tests for:\n- API endpoints\n- Database operations\n- External service integrations\n\nUse `@SpringBootTest` for integration tests.\n\n#### Running Tests\n\n```bash\n# All tests\n./gradlew test\n\n# Specific module\n./gradlew :domain:domain-order:test\n\n# With coverage\n./gradlew test jacocoTestReport\n```\n\n### Frontend Testing\n\n#### Component Tests\n\nWrite tests for:\n- Component rendering\n- User interactions\n- Edge cases and error states\n\nExample with Vitest and Testing Library:\n```typescript\nimport { render, screen, fireEvent } from '@testing-library/react';\nimport { describe, it, expect } from 'vitest';\nimport { OrderList } from './OrderList';\n\ndescribe('OrderList', () => {\n  it('renders orders when data is loaded', () => {\n    render(<OrderList />);\n    expect(screen.getByText('Order #1')).toBeInTheDocument();\n  });\n\n  it('handles order selection', () => {\n    render(<OrderList />);\n    fireEvent.click(screen.getByText('Order #1'));\n    expect(screen.getByText('Selected')).toBeInTheDocument();\n  });\n});\n```\n\n#### Hook Tests\n\nTest custom hooks with `@testing-library/react-hooks`.\n\n#### Running Tests\n\n```bash\n# All tests\npnpm test\n\n# Watch mode\npnpm test:watch\n\n# Coverage\npnpm test:coverage\n\n# UI mode\npnpm test:ui\n```\n\n### Test Coverage Requirements\n\n- **Backend**: Minimum 80% line coverage for new code\n- **Frontend**: Minimum 70% line coverage for new code\n- **Critical Paths**: 100% coverage for payment, inventory, settlement\n\n## Code Review Process\n\n### As a Contributor\n\n- Respond to feedback promptly\n- Be open to suggestions\n- Ask questions if feedback is unclear\n- Update the PR based on feedback\n- Mark conversations as resolved when addressed\n\n### As a Reviewer\n\n- Be respectful and constructive\n- Explain the \"why\" behind suggestions\n- Distinguish between blocking and non-blocking feedback\n- Use GitHub's suggestion feature for minor changes\n- Approve when satisfied or request changes\n\n### Review Checklist\n\n- [ ] Code follows project conventions\n- [ ] Logic is clear and well-structured\n- [ ] Tests are comprehensive\n- [ ] Documentation is updated\n- [ ] No obvious bugs or security issues\n- [ ] Performance is acceptable\n- [ ] No unnecessary dependencies added\n\n## Need Help?\n\n- **Documentation**: Check README.md, ARCHITECTURE.md\n- **Issues**: Browse existing issues or create a new one\n- **Discussions**: Use GitHub Discussions for questions\n- **Code of Conduct**: Be respectful and inclusive\n\n## License\n\nBy contributing, you agree that your contributions will be licensed under the MIT License.\n\nThank you for contributing to Global OMS!\n"
}

{
  "file_path": "/Users/sonmingi/.openclaw/workspace/issue-pilot/.repos/order-management-system/backend/BACKEND.md",
  "content": "# Backend - Global OMS\n\nThis document provides detailed documentation for the Global OMS backend.\n\n## Table of Contents\n\n- [Overview](#overview)\n- [Technology Stack](#technology-stack)\n- [Architecture](#architecture)\n- [Module Structure](#module-structure)\n- [Bounded Contexts](#bounded-contexts)\n- [Development](#development)\n- [Database](#database)\n- [API Documentation](#api-documentation)\n- [Testing](#testing)\n- [Code Quality](#code-quality)\n- [Deployment](#deployment)\n\n## Overview\n\nThe Global OMS backend is built using Domain-Driven Design (DDD) principles with Kotlin and Spring Boot. It leverages JDK 21's Virtual Threads for improved concurrency and uses PostgreSQL as the primary database with MongoDB for flexible schemas.\n\n## Technology Stack\n\n- **Language**: Kotlin 1.9\n- **Runtime**: JDK 21 (Virtual Threads enabled)\n- **Framework**: Spring Boot 3.2\n- **Databases**:\n  - PostgreSQL 16 (primary RDBMS)\n  - MongoDB 7.0 (documents, events)\n  - Redis 7 (caching)\n- **Build Tool**: Gradle 8.5\n- **Testing**: JUnit 5, MockK, Testcontainers\n- **Code Quality**: detekt, ktlint\n- **API Documentation**: SpringDoc OpenAPI (Swagger)\n\n## Architecture\n\n### Layered Architecture\n\n```\n┌─────────────────────────────────────┐\n│        API Layer (api)              │\n│  - REST Controllers                 │\n│  - Request/Response DTOs            │\n│  - Exception Handlers               │\n└─────────────────────────────────────┘\n              ▼\n┌─────────────────────────────────────┐\n│   Application Layer (application)   │\n│  - Application Services             │\n│  - Use Cases                        │\n│  - Event Handlers                   │\n└─────────────────────────────────────┘\n              ▼\n┌─────────────────────────────────────┐\n│     Domain Layer (domain)           │\n│  - Entities & Value Objects         │\n│  - Domain Services                  │\n│  - Repository Interfaces            │\n│  - Domain Events                    │\n└─────────────────────────────────────┘\n              ▼\n┌─────────────────────────────────────┐\n│  Infrastructure Layer (infra)       │\n│  - JPA Repositories (PostgreSQL)    │\n│  - MongoDB Repositories             │\n│  - Redis Cache                      │\n│  - External Service Clients         │\n└─────────────────────────────────────┘\n```\n\n### Hexagonal Architecture\n\nThe backend follows hexagonal architecture (ports and adapters):\n\n- **Domain**: Core business logic (independent of frameworks)\n- **Ports**: Interfaces for inbound/outbound communication\n- **Adapters**: Implementations of ports (REST API, JPA, etc.)\n\n## Module Structure\n\n```\nbackend/\n├── api/                           # REST API layer\n│   ├── src/main/kotlin/\n│   │   └── com/globaloms/api/\n│   │       ├── config/            # Spring configuration\n│   │       ├── controller/        # REST controllers\n│   │       ├── dto/               # Request/Response DTOs\n│   │       └── exception/         # Global exception handling\n│   └── build.gradle.kts\n│\n├── application/                   # Application services\n│   ├── src/main/kotlin/\n│   │   └── com/globaloms/application/\n│   │       ├── order/             # Order use cases\n│   │       ├── inventory/         # Inventory use cases\n│   │       ├── channel/           # Channel use cases\n│   │       └── ...\n│   └── build.gradle.kts\n│\n├── domain/                        # Domain modules (bounded contexts)\n│   ├── domain-order/              # Order context\n│   ├── domain-inventory/          # Inventory context\n│   ├── domain-channel/            # Channel context\n│   ├── domain-claim/              # Claim context\n│   ├── domain-settlement/         # Settlement context\n│   ├── domain-automation/         # Automation context\n│   ├── domain-strategy/           # Strategy context\n│   ├── domain-catalog/            # Catalog context\n│   └── domain-identity/           # Identity context\n│\n├── infrastructure/                # Infrastructure implementations\n│   ├── infra-postgres/            # JPA repositories (PostgreSQL)\n│   ├── infra-mongo/               # MongoDB repositories\n│   └── infra-redis/               # Redis cache\n│\n└── core/\n    └── core-domain/               # Shared domain\n        ├── entity/                # Base entities\n        ├── event/                 # Domain events\n        └── common/                # Common utilities\n```\n\n## Bounded Contexts\n\n### 1. Order Context (`domain-order`)\n\n**Responsibility**: Manages the complete order lifecycle.\n\n**Key Entities**:\n- `Order`: Main order aggregate\n- `OrderItem`: Items within an order\n- `OrderStatus`: Order state enumeration\n\n**Key Operations**:\n- Create order\n- Update order status\n- Cancel order\n- Split/merge orders\n\n**Events**:\n- `OrderCreatedEvent`\n- `OrderConfirmedEvent`\n- `OrderCancelledEvent`\n\n### 2. Channel Context (`domain-channel`)\n\n**Responsibility**: Multi-channel sales management.\n\n**Key Entities**:\n- `Channel`: Sales channel (marketplace, own store)\n- `Warehouse`: Fulfillment center\n- `ChannelPolicy`: Channel-specific rules\n\n**Key Operations**:\n- Register channel\n- Manage warehouses\n- Configure channel policies\n\n**Events**:\n- `ChannelRegisteredEvent`\n- `WarehouseCreatedEvent`\n\n### 3. Inventory Context (`domain-inventory`)\n\n**Responsibility**: Stock management across warehouses.\n\n**Key Entities**:\n- `Stock`: Inventory item\n- `StockReservation`: Reserved inventory\n- `StockMovement`: Inventory history\n\n**Key Operations**:\n- Check availability\n- Reserve stock\n- Release reservation\n- Update stock levels\n\n**Events**:\n- `StockReservedEvent`\n- `StockReleasedEvent`\n- `StockLevelChangedEvent`\n\n### 4. Claim Context (`domain-claim`)\n\n**Responsibility**: Returns, exchanges, and refunds.\n\n**Key Entities**:\n- `Claim`: Claim aggregate\n- `ClaimType`: Return/Exchange/Refund\n- `ClaimStatus`: Claim state\n\n**Key Operations**:\n- Create claim\n- Process claim\n- Approve/reject claim\n\n**Events**:\n- `ClaimCreatedEvent`\n- `ClaimApprovedEvent`\n- `RefundProcessedEvent`\n\n### 5. Settlement Context (`domain-settlement`)\n\n**Responsibility**: Financial settlement processing.\n\n**Key Entities**:\n- `Settlement`: Settlement aggregate\n- `SettlementItem`: Individual settlement entry\n- `FeePolicy`: Fee calculation rules\n\n**Key Operations**:\n- Calculate settlement\n- Generate settlement report\n- Process payment\n\n**Events**:\n- `SettlementCalculatedEvent`\n- `PaymentProcessedEvent`\n\n### 6. Automation Context (`domain-automation`)\n\n**Responsibility**: Rule-based automation.\n\n**Key Entities**:\n- `AutomationRule`: Conditional rule\n- `Action`: Automated action\n- `Trigger`: Rule activation condition\n\n**Key Operations**:\n- Create automation rule\n- Execute rule\n- Enable/disable rule\n\n### 7. Strategy Context (`domain-strategy`)\n\n**Responsibility**: Operational strategies and readiness.\n\n**Key Entities**:\n- `AllocationStrategy`: Inventory distribution strategy\n- `GlobalReadiness`: Operational readiness status\n\n**Key Operations**:\n- Define allocation strategy\n- Check readiness status\n\n### 8. Catalog Context (`domain-catalog`)\n\n**Responsibility**: Product information management.\n\n**Key Entities**:\n- `Product`: Product aggregate\n- `SKU`: Stock keeping unit\n- `Category`: Product categorization\n\n**Key Operations**:\n- Create product\n- Update product info\n- Manage SKU\n\n**Events**:\n- `ProductCreatedEvent`\n- `ProductUpdatedEvent`\n\n### 9. Identity Context (`domain-identity`)\n\n**Responsibility**: User and organization management.\n\n**Key Entities**:\n- `Company`: Organization/tenant\n- `User`: User account\n- `Role`: User role\n- `Permission`: Access permission\n\n**Key Operations**:\n- Register company\n- Create user\n- Assign roles\n- Check permissions\n\n**Events**:\n- `CompanyRegisteredEvent`\n- `UserCreatedEvent`\n\n## Development\n\n### Prerequisites\n\n- JDK 21+ (with Virtual Threads)\n- Docker Desktop (for local infrastructure)\n- IntelliJ IDEA (recommended) or any Kotlin IDE\n\n### Setup\n\n1. **Clone the repository**:\n   ```bash\n   git clone https://github.com/smk692/order-management-system.git\n   cd order-management-system/backend\n   ```\n\n2. **Start infrastructure**:\n   ```bash\n   # From project root\n   docker compose -f docker-compose.dev.yml up -d\n   ```\n\n3. **Build the project**:\n   ```bash\n   ./gradlew build\n   ```\n\n4. **Run the application**:\n   ```bash\n   ./gradlew :api:bootRun\n   ```\n\n5. **Access Swagger UI**:\n   Open http://localhost:8080/swagger-ui/\n\n### Gradle Tasks\n\n```bash\n# Build all modules\n./gradlew build\n\n# Run API server\n./gradlew :api:bootRun\n\n# Run tests\n./gradlew test\n\n# Run tests for specific module\n./gradlew :domain:domain-order:test\n\n# Code quality checks\n./gradlew ktlintCheck detekt\n\n# Format code\n./gradlew ktlintFormat\n\n# Generate test coverage report\n./gradlew test jacocoTestReport\n\n# Clean build artifacts\n./gradlew clean\n```\n\n### IntelliJ IDEA Setup\n\n1. **Import Project**: File → Open → Select `backend` directory\n2. **Enable Kotlin**: IntelliJ should auto-detect Kotlin\n3. **Configure JDK**: File → Project Structure → Project SDK → JDK 21\n4. **Enable Virtual Threads**: Already configured in `application.yml`\n\n## Database\n\n### PostgreSQL\n\n**Primary RDBMS** for transactional data.\n\n**Schema Initialization**:\n- Located in `docker/postgres/init/init.sql`\n- Creates database and schema on container startup\n\n**Connection Configuration**:\n```yaml\n# application.yml\nspring:\n  datasource:\n    url: jdbc:postgresql://localhost:5432/oms\n    username: oms\n    password: oms_password\n```\n\n**JPA Configuration**:\n```yaml\nspring:\n  jpa:\n    hibernate:\n      ddl-auto: validate  # Use Flyway/Liquibase for migrations\n    show-sql: false\n    properties:\n      hibernate:\n        format_sql: true\n        dialect: org.hibernate.dialect.PostgreSQLDialect\n```\n\n### MongoDB\n\n**Document Store** for flexible schemas (events, logs, analytics).\n\n**Connection Configuration**:\n```yaml\n# application.yml\nspring:\n  data:\n    mongodb:\n      uri: mongodb://oms:oms_password@localhost:27017/oms\n      database: oms\n```\n\n**Usage Example**:\n```kotlin\n@Document(collection = \"order_events\")\ndata class OrderEventDocument(\n    @Id val id: String? = null,\n    val orderId: String,\n    val eventType: String,\n    val payload: Map<String, Any>,\n    val timestamp: Instant\n)\n```\n\n### Redis\n\n**Cache Layer** for frequently accessed data.\n\n**Connection Configuration**:\n```yaml\n# application.yml\nspring:\n  data:\n    redis:\n      host: localhost\n      port: 6379\n```\n\n**Usage Example**:\n```kotlin\n@Cacheable(value = [\"products\"], key = \"#productId\")\nfun getProduct(productId: String): Product {\n    // Fetches from database if not in cache\n}\n```\n\n### Database Migrations\n\n**Recommended Tool**: Flyway or Liquibase (to be configured)\n\n**Migration Structure**:\n```\nresources/db/migration/\n├── V1__initial_schema.sql\n├── V2__add_claim_tables.sql\n└── V3__add_indexes.sql\n```\n\n## API Documentation\n\n### Swagger/OpenAPI\n\n- **Swagger UI**: http://localhost:8080/swagger-ui/\n- **OpenAPI JSON**: http://localhost:8080/v3/api-docs\n\n### API Versioning\n\nAll APIs are versioned with `/api/v1` prefix.\n\n### Example Endpoints\n\n```bash\n# Get all orders\nGET /api/v1/orders\n\n# Get specific order\nGET /api/v1/orders/{orderId}\n\n# Create order\nPOST /api/v1/orders\n\n# Update order status\nPATCH /api/v1/orders/{orderId}/status\n\n# Cancel order\nPOST /api/v1/orders/{orderId}/cancel\n```\n\n### Request/Response Examples\n\n**Create Order**:\n```json\nPOST /api/v1/orders\n{\n  \"customerId\": \"cust-123\",\n  \"items\": [\n    {\n      \"productId\": \"prod-456\",\n      \"quantity\": 2,\n      \"price\": 29.99\n    }\n  ],\n  \"shippingAddress\": {\n    \"street\": \"123 Main St\",\n    \"city\": \"Seoul\",\n    \"country\": \"KR\"\n  }\n}\n```\n\n**Response**:\n```json\n{\n  \"orderId\": \"ord-789\",\n  \"status\": \"CREATED\",\n  \"totalAmount\": 59.98,\n  \"createdAt\": \"2024-01-15T10:30:00Z\"\n}\n```\n\n## Testing\n\n### Unit Tests\n\n**Framework**: JUnit 5, MockK\n\n**Example**:\n```kotlin\n@Test\nfun `should create order when inventory is sufficient`() {\n    // Given\n    val createOrderCommand = CreateOrderCommand(...)\n    every { inventoryService.checkAvailability(...) } returns true\n\n    // When\n    val result = orderService.createOrder(createOrderCommand)\n\n    // Then\n    assertThat(result.status).isEqualTo(OrderStatus.CREATED)\n    verify { inventoryService.reserveStock(...) }\n}\n```\n\n### Integration Tests\n\n**Framework**: Spring Boot Test, Testcontainers\n\n**Example**:\n```kotlin\n@SpringBootTest\n@Testcontainers\nclass OrderIntegrationTest {\n\n    @Container\n    val postgres = PostgreSQLContainer<Nothing>(\"postgres:16\")\n\n    @Test\n    fun `should persist order to database`() {\n        // Test with real database via Testcontainers\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### Running Tests\n\n```bash\n# All tests\n./gradlew test\n\n# Specific module\n./gradlew :domain:domain-order:test\n\n# With coverage\n./gradlew test jacocoTestReport\n\n# Open coverage report\nopen build/reports/jacoco/test/html/index.html\n```\n\n## Code Quality\n\n### ktlint\n\n**Kotlin Style Enforcement**\n\nConfiguration: `.editorconfig`\n\n```bash\n# Check style\n./gradlew ktlintCheck\n\n# Auto-format\n./gradlew ktlintFormat\n```\n\n### detekt\n\n**Static Code Analysis**\n\nConfiguration: `detekt.yml`\n\n```bash\n# Run detekt\n./gradlew detekt\n\n# View report\nopen build/reports/detekt/detekt.html\n```\n\n### Running All Checks\n\n```bash\n# Format, lint, analyze, and test\n./gradlew ktlintFormat detekt test\n```\n\n## Deployment\n\n### Docker Build\n\n```bash\n# Build backend Docker image\ndocker build -t global-oms-backend:latest -f docker/backend/Dockerfile .\n\n# Run with Docker Compose\ndocker compose up -d\n```\n\n### Environment Variables\n\n```bash\n# Database\nPOSTGRES_HOST=localhost\nPOSTGRES_PORT=5432\nPOSTGRES_DB=oms\nPOSTGRES_USER=oms\nPOSTGRES_PASSWORD=oms_password\n\n# MongoDB\nMONGO_HOST=localhost\nMONGO_PORT=27017\nMONGO_DATABASE=oms\nMONGO_USER=oms\nMONGO_PASSWORD=oms_password\n\n# Redis\nREDIS_HOST=localhost\nREDIS_PORT=6379\n\n# Application\nSERVER_PORT=8080\nSPRING_PROFILES_ACTIVE=dev\n```\n\n### Production Checklist\n\n- [ ] Set `spring.profiles.active=prod`\n- [ ] Enable HTTPS\n- [ ] Configure proper database credentials\n- [ ] Set up database backups\n- [ ] Configure logging (centralized)\n- [ ] Enable monitoring (Actuator endpoints)\n- [ ] Set up APM (Application Performance Monitoring)\n- [ ] Configure rate limiting\n- [ ] Enable CORS properly\n- [ ] Review security headers\n\n## JDK 21 Virtual Threads\n\n### Configuration\n\nVirtual Threads are enabled in `application.yml`:\n\n```yaml\nspring:\n  threads:\n    virtual:\n      enabled: true\n```\n\n### Benefits\n\n- **Lightweight**: Millions of virtual threads vs. thousands of OS threads\n- **Simplified Concurrency**: No need for reactive programming\n- **Backward Compatible**: Works with existing blocking code\n\n### Usage\n\nNo code changes needed. Spring Boot automatically uses virtual threads for:\n- Request handling\n- `@Async` methods\n- `ExecutorService` beans\n\n## Best Practices\n\n### Domain Layer\n\n- Keep domain logic in domain modules\n- Use aggregates to enforce consistency\n- Emit domain events for cross-context communication\n- Use value objects for immutability\n\n### Application Layer\n\n- Application services orchestrate domain logic\n- Handle transactions at the application layer\n- Convert between domain models and DTOs\n\n### Infrastructure Layer\n\n- Repository implementations should be thin\n- Don't leak infrastructure details to domain\n- Use interfaces for external dependencies\n\n### API Layer\n\n- Validate input at the controller level\n- Use DTOs for request/response\n- Handle exceptions globally\n- Document APIs with Swagger annotations\n\n## Troubleshooting\n\n### Common Issues\n\n**Database Connection Failed**:\n```bash\n# Ensure infrastructure is running\ndocker compose -f docker-compose.dev.yml ps\n\n# Check PostgreSQL\ndocker compose -f docker-compose.dev.yml logs postgres\n```\n\n**Build Failed**:\n```bash\n# Clean and rebuild\n./gradlew clean build --refresh-dependencies\n```\n\n**Tests Failed**:\n```bash\n# Run tests with stack traces\n./gradlew test --stacktrace\n```\n\n## Further Reading\n\n- [Spring Boot Documentation](https://docs.spring.io/spring-boot/docs/current/reference/html/)\n- [Kotlin Official Docs](https://kotlinlang.org/docs/home.html)\n- [JDK 21 Virtual Threads](https://openjdk.org/jeps/444)\n- [Domain-Driven Design](https://martinfowler.com/tags/domain%20driven%20design.html)\n"
}
```

{
  "file_path": "/Users/sonmingi/.openclaw/workspace/issue-pilot/.repos/order-management-system/frontend/FRONTEND.md",
  "content": "# Frontend - Global OMS\n\nThis document provides detailed documentation for the Global OMS frontend.\n\n## Table of Contents\n\n- [Overview](#overview)\n- [Technology Stack](#technology-stack)\n- [Architecture](#architecture)\n- [Project Structure](#project-structure)\n- [State Management](#state-management)\n- [Development](#development)\n- [Styling](#styling)\n- [Testing](#testing)\n- [Code Quality](#code-quality)\n- [Build and Deployment](#build-and-deployment)\n\n## Overview\n\nThe Global OMS frontend is a modern React application built with TypeScript, Vite, and feature-based architecture. It uses React Query for server state management and Zustand for UI state, providing a clear separation of concerns.\n\n## Technology Stack\n\n- **Language**: TypeScript 5+\n- **Framework**: React 19\n- **Build Tool**: Vite 6\n- **Package Manager**: pnpm 9+\n- **State Management**:\n  - React Query (TanStack Query) - Server state\n  - Zustand - UI state\n- **Routing**: React Router 7\n- **Styling**: CSS Modules / Tailwind CSS (to be configured)\n- **Testing**: Vitest, Testing Library\n- **Code Quality**: ESLint 9, Prettier\n- **Internationalization**: i18next\n\n## Architecture\n\n### Feature-Based Architecture\n\nThe frontend follows a feature-based architecture where code is organized by business feature rather than technical layer.\n\n```\nsrc/\n├── features/              # Feature modules\n│   ├── orders/            # Order management feature\n│   │   ├── components/    # Order-specific components\n│   │   ├── hooks/         # Order-related hooks\n│   │   ├── api/           # Order API calls (React Query)\n│   │   ├── store/         # Order UI state (Zustand)\n│   │   ├── types/         # Order TypeScript types\n│   │   └── index.ts       # Public exports\n│   ├── inventory/\n│   ├── channels/\n│   └── ...\n├── components/            # Shared components\n│   └── ui/                # Reusable UI components\n├── lib/                   # Shared utilities\n│   ├── api/               # API client setup\n│   ├── query/             # React Query configuration\n│   └── i18n/              # i18n configuration\n├── hooks/                 # Shared hooks\n├── types/                 # Shared TypeScript types\n└── App.tsx                # Root component\n```\n\n### Component Hierarchy\n\n```\nApp\n├── Layout\n│   ├── Header\n│   ├── Sidebar\n│   └── Content\n│       ├── OrderListPage (Feature)\n│       │   ├── OrderList (Feature Component)\n│       │   │   ├── OrderItem\n│       │   │   └── OrderFilters\n│       │   └── OrderDetail (Feature Component)\n│       └── InventoryPage (Feature)\n```\n\n## Project Structure\n\n### Feature Module Structure\n\nEach feature follows a consistent structure:\n\n```\nfeatures/orders/\n├── components/            # UI components\n│   ├── OrderList.tsx\n│   ├── OrderDetail.tsx\n│   ├── OrderForm.tsx\n│   └── index.ts\n├── hooks/                 # Custom hooks\n│   ├── useOrders.ts       # React Query hook\n│   ├── useOrderForm.ts    # Form logic\n│   └── index.ts\n├── api/                   # API calls\n│   ├── orderApi.ts        # React Query queries/mutations\n│   └── index.ts\n├── store/                 # UI state (Zustand)\n│   ├── orderStore.ts\n│   └── index.ts\n├── types/                 # TypeScript types\n│   ├── order.ts\n│   └── index.ts\n├── utils/                 # Feature utilities\n│   ├── orderUtils.ts\n│   └── index.ts\n└── index.ts               # Public exports\n```\n\n### Shared Components\n\n```\ncomponents/ui/\n├── Button/\n│   ├── Button.tsx\n│   ├── Button.test.tsx\n│   ├── Button.module.css\n│   └── index.ts\n├── Input/\n├── Modal/\n├── Table/\n└── ...\n```\n\n## State Management\n\n### React Query (Server State)\n\n**Purpose**: Manage server-synchronized data (API responses).\n\n**Features**:\n- Automatic caching\n- Background refetching\n- Optimistic updates\n- Request deduplication\n- Pagination and infinite scroll\n\n**Setup** (`lib/query/queryClient.ts`):\n```typescript\nimport { QueryClient } from '@tanstack/react-query';\n\nexport const queryClient = new QueryClient({\n  defaultOptions: {\n    queries: {\n      staleTime: 1000 * 60 * 5, // 5 minutes\n      retry: 1,\n      refetchOnWindowFocus: false,\n    },\n  },\n});\n```\n\n**Usage Example** (`features/orders/hooks/useOrders.ts`):\n```typescript\nimport { useQuery, useMutation, useQueryClient } from '@tanstack/react-query';\nimport { orderApi } from '../api/orderApi';\n\nexport function useOrders() {\n  return useQuery({\n    queryKey: ['orders'],\n    queryFn: orderApi.getOrders,\n  });\n}\n\nexport function useCreateOrder() {\n  const queryClient = useQueryClient();\n\n  return useMutation({\n    mutationFn: orderApi.createOrder,\n    onSuccess: () => {\n      // Invalidate and refetch orders\n      queryClient.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ['orders'] });\n    },\n  });\n}\n```\n\n**Component Usage**:\n```typescript\nfunction OrderList() {\n  const { data, isLoading, error } = useOrders();\n  const createOrder = useCreateOrder();\n\n  if (isLoading) return <LoadingSpinner />;\n  if (error) return <ErrorMessage error={error} />;\n\n  return (\n    <div>\n      {data?.map(order => <OrderItem key={order.id} order={order} />)}\n      <button onClick={() => createOrder.mutate(newOrder)}>\n        Create Order\n      </button>\n    </div>\n  );\n}\n```\n\n### Zustand (UI State)\n\n**Purpose**: Manage local UI state (modals, forms, selections).\n\n**Features**:\n- Simple and lightweight\n- No boilerplate\n- DevTools support\n- TypeScript-friendly\n\n**Setup** (`features/orders/store/orderStore.ts`):\n```typescript\nimport { create } from 'zustand';\nimport { devtools } from 'zustand/middleware';\n\ninterface OrderStore {\n  selectedOrderId: string | null;\n  isModalOpen: boolean;\n  setSelectedOrderId: (id: string | null) => void;\n  openModal: () => void;\n  closeModal: () => void;\n}\n\nexport const useOrderStore = create<OrderStore>()(\n  devtools(\n    (set) => ({\n      selectedOrderId: null,\n      isModalOpen: false,\n      setSelectedOrderId: (id) => set({ selectedOrderId: id }),\n      openModal: () => set({ isModalOpen: true }),\n      closeModal: () => set({ isModalOpen: false }),\n    }),\n    { name: 'OrderStore' }\n  )\n);\n```\n\n**Component Usage**:\n```typescript\nfunction OrderList() {\n  const { selectedOrderId, setSelectedOrderId } = useOrderStore();\n\n  return (\n    <div>\n      {orders.map(order => (\n        <OrderItem\n          key={order.id}\n          order={order}\n          isSelected={order.id === selectedOrderId}\n          onClick={() => setSelectedOrderId(order.id)}\n        />\n      ))}\n    </div>\n  );\n}\n```\n\n### State Management Decision Tree\n\n```\n┌─ Is this data from an API?\n│  ├─ YES → Use React Query\n│  └─ NO → Continue\n│\n└─ Does this state need to be shared across multiple components?\n   ├─ YES → Use Zustand\n   └─ NO → Use local component state (useState)\n```\n\n## Development\n\n### Prerequisites\n\n- Node.js 20+\n- pnpm 9+\n\n### Setup\n\n1. **Install dependencies**:\n   ```bash\n   cd frontend\n   pnpm install\n   ```\n\n2. **Start development server**:\n   ```bash\n   pnpm dev\n   ```\n\n3. **Access the app**:\n   Open http://localhost:3000\n\n### Package Scripts\n\n```bash\n# Development\npnpm dev               # Start dev server with HMR\npnpm dev:host          # Expose to network\n\n# Building\npnpm build             # Production build\npnpm preview           # Preview production build\n\n# Testing\npnpm test              # Run tests in watch mode\npnpm test:run          # Run tests once\npnpm test:coverage     # Generate coverage report\npnpm test:ui           # Open Vitest UI\n\n# Code Quality\npnpm lint              # Lint with ESLint\npnpm lint:fix          # Auto-fix lint issues\npnpm format            # Format with Prettier\npnpm format:check      # Check formatting\npnpm type-check        # TypeScript type checking\n\n# All Checks\npnpm check-all         # Run lint, format:check, type-check, test\n```\n\n### Environment Variables\n\nCreate `.env.local` for local overrides:\n\n```bash\nVITE_API_BASE_URL=http://localhost:8080/api/v1\nVITE_WS_URL=ws://localhost:8080/ws\nVITE_APP_TITLE=Global OMS\n```\n\nAccess in code:\n```typescript\nconst apiBaseUrl = import.meta.env.VITE_API_BASE_URL;\n```\n\n## Styling\n\n### CSS Modules (Current)\n\nEach component has its own CSS module:\n\n```typescript\n// Button.tsx\nimport styles from './Button.module.css';\n\nexport function Button({ children }: ButtonProps) {\n  return <button className={styles.button}>{children}</button>;\n}\n```\n\n```css\n/* Button.module.css */\n.button {\n  padding: 0.5rem 1rem;\n  background-color: #007bff;\n  color: white;\n  border: none;\n  border-radius: 4px;\n}\n```\n\n### Tailwind CSS (Planned)\n\nTo be configured for utility-first CSS:\n\n```typescript\nexport function Button({ children }: ButtonProps) {\n  return (\n    <button className=\"px-4 py-2 bg-blue-500 text-white rounded hover:bg-blue-600\">\n      {children}\n    </button>\n  );\n}\n```\n\n### Styling Best Practices\n\n- Use semantic class names\n- Keep styles scoped to components\n- Avoid global styles except for resets/base styles\n- Use CSS custom properties for theming\n\n## Testing\n\n### Testing Framework\n\n- **Vitest**: Fast unit test runner\n- **Testing Library**: React component testing\n- **MSW** (Planned): Mock Service Worker for API mocking\n\n### Unit Tests\n\nTest component logic and hooks:\n\n```typescript\n// Button.test.tsx\nimport { render, screen, fireEvent } from '@testing-library/react';\nimport { describe, it, expect, vi } from 'vitest';\nimport { Button } from './Button';\n\ndescribe('Button', () => {\n  it('renders children', () => {\n    render(<Button>Click me</Button>);\n    expect(screen.getByText('Click me')).toBeInTheDocument();\n  });\n\n  it('calls onClick when clicked', () => {\n    const handleClick = vi.fn();\n    render(<Button onClick={handleClick}>Click me</Button>);\n\n    fireEvent.click(screen.getByText('Click me'));\n    expect(handleClick).toHaveBeenCalledTimes(1);\n  });\n});\n```\n\n### Integration Tests\n\nTest feature workflows:\n\n```typescript\n// OrderList.test.tsx\nimport { render, screen, waitFor } from '@testing-library/react';\nimport { QueryClientProvider } from '@tanstack/react-query';\nimport { OrderList } from './OrderList';\nimport { queryClient } from '@/lib/query/queryClient';\n\ndescribe('OrderList', () => {\n  it('displays orders when loaded', async () => {\n    render(\n      <QueryClientProvider client={queryClient}>\n        <OrderList />\n      </QueryClientProvider>\n    );\n\n    await waitFor(() => {\n      expect(screen.getByText('Order #1')).toBeInTheDocument();\n    });\n  });\n});\n```\n\n### Hook Tests\n\nTest custom hooks:\n\n```typescript\n// useOrders.test.ts\nimport { renderHook, waitFor } from '@testing-library/react';\nimport { QueryClientProvider } from '@tanstack/react-query';\nimport { useOrders } from './useOrders';\n\ndescribe('useOrders', () => {\n  it('fetches orders successfully', async () => {\n    const { result } = renderHook(() => useOrders(), {\n      wrapper: QueryClientProvider,\n    });\n\n    await waitFor(() => expect(result.current.isSuccess).toBe(true));\n    expect(result.current.data).toHaveLength(3);\n  });\n});\n```\n\n### Running Tests\n\n```bash\n# Watch mode (default)\npnpm test\n\n# Run once\npnpm test:run\n\n# Coverage report\npnpm test:coverage\n\n# UI mode\npnpm test:ui\n```\n\n### Test Coverage Goals\n\n- **Components**: >70% coverage\n- **Hooks**: >80% coverage\n- **Utilities**: >90% coverage\n\n## Code Quality\n\n### ESLint 9 (Flat Config)\n\nConfiguration: `eslint.config.js`\n\n```javascript\nimport js from '@eslint/js';\nimport typescript from '@typescript-eslint/eslint-plugin';\nimport react from 'eslint-plugin-react';\nimport reactHooks from 'eslint-plugin-react-hooks';\n\nexport default [\n  js.configs.recommended,\n  {\n    files: ['**/*.{ts,tsx}'],\n    plugins: {\n      '@typescript-eslint': typescript,\n      react,\n      'react-hooks': reactHooks,\n    },\n    rules: {\n      'react-hooks/rules-of-hooks': 'error',\n      'react-hooks/exhaustive-deps': 'warn',\n      '@typescript-eslint/no-unused-vars': 'warn',\n    },\n  },\n];\n```\n\n**Run**:\n```bash\npnpm lint\npnpm lint:fix\n```\n\n### Prettier\n\nConfiguration:  \"lib\": [\"ES2020\", \"DOM\", \"DOM.Iterable\"],\n    \"module\": \"ESNext\",\n    \"moduleResolution\": \"bundler\",\n    \"strict\": true,\n    \"jsx\": \"react-jsx\",\n    \"paths\": {\n      \"@/*\": [\"./src/*\"]\n    }\n  }\n}\n```\n\n**Run**:\n```bash\npnpm type-check\n```\n\n### Pre-commit Checks\n\nRun all checks before committing:\n\n```bash\npnpm check-all\n# Runs: lint, format:check, type-check, test\n```\n\n## Build and Deployment\n\n### Production Build\n\n```bash\n# Build for production\npnpm build\n\n# Preview production build\npnpm preview\n```\n\nBuild output: `dist/`\n\n### Docker Build\n\n```bash\n# Build Docker image\ndocker build -t global-oms-frontend:latest -f docker/frontend/Dockerfile .\n\n# Run with Docker Compose\ndocker compose up -d\n```\n\n### Environment-Specific Builds\n\n```bash\n# Development\npnpm build --mode development\n\n# Staging\npnpm build --mode staging\n\n# Production\npnpm build --mode production\n```\n\n### Bundle Analysis\n\n```bash\n# Analyze bundle size (to be configured)\npnpm build --analyze\n```\n\n### Deployment Checklist\n\n- [ ] Run `pnpm check-all` (lint, format, type-check, test)\n- [ ] Run `pnpm build` successfully\n- [ ] Test production build with `pnpm preview`\n- [ ] Verify environment variables are set\n- [ ] Check bundle size is acceptable\n- [ ] Ensure HTTPS is configured\n- [ ] Configure CORS for API\n- [ ] Set up error tracking (Sentry)\n- [ ] Enable analytics (optional)\n\n## Internationalization (i18n)\n\n### Setup with i18next\n\nConfiguration: `lib/i18n/i18n.ts`\n\n```typescript\nimport i18n from 'i18next';\nimport { initReactI18next } from 'react-i18next';\nimport en from './locales/en.json';\nimport ko from './locales/ko.json';\n\ni18n.use(initReactI18next).init({\n  resources: {\n    en: { translation: en },\n    ko: { translation: ko },\n  },\n  lng: 'en',\n  fallbackLng: 'en',\n  interpolation: {\n    escapeValue: false,\n  },\n});\n\nexport default i18n;\n```\n\n### Usage in Components\n\n```typescript\nimport { useTranslation } from 'react-i18next';\n\nexport function OrderList() {\n  const { t } = useTranslation();\n\n  return (\n    <div>\n      <h1>{t('orders.title')}</h1>\n      <p>{t('orders.description')}</p>\n    </div>\n  );\n}\n```\n\n### Translation Files\n\n```json\n// locales/en.json\n{\n  \"orders\": {\n    \"title\": \"Orders\",\n    \"description\": \"Manage your orders\"\n  }\n}\n\n// locales/ko.json\n{\n  \"orders\": {\n    \"title\": \"주문\",\n    \"description\": \"주문을 관리하세요\"\n  }\n}\n```\n\n## Best Practices\n\n### Component Design\n\n- **Single Responsibility**: One component, one purpose\n- **Composition**: Build complex UIs from small components\n- **Props**: Keep props simple and typed\n- **Hooks**: Extract logic into custom hooks\n\n### State Management\n\n- **Server State**: Always use React Query for API data\n- **UI State**: Use Zustand for shared UI state\n- **Local State**: Use `useState` for component-specific state\n\n### Performance\n\n- **Code Splitting**: Use `React.lazy()` for route-based splitting\n- **Memoization**: Use `useMemo` and `useCallback` judiciously\n- **React Query**: Leverage caching to reduce API calls\n- **Avoid Re-renders**: Use `React.memo()` for expensive components\n\n### Accessibility\n\n- Use semantic HTML elements\n- Add ARIA attributes when needed\n- Ensure keyboard navigation works\n- Test with screen readers\n\n### Security\n\n- Validate user input\n- Sanitize HTML to prevent XSS\n- Use HTTPS in production\n- Don't store sensitive data in localStorage\n\n## Troubleshooting\n\n### Common Issues\n\n**Development server not starting**:\n```bash\n# Clear node_modules and reinstall\nrm -rf node_modules\npnpm install\n```\n\n**Type errors**:\n```bash\n# Re-run type checking\npnpm type-check\n```\n\n**Build fails**:\n```bash\n# Clean and rebuild\nrm -rf dist\npnpm build\n```\n\n**Tests failing**:\n```bash\n# Run tests with verbose output\npnpm test:run --reporter=verbose\n```\n\n## Further Reading\n\n- [React Documentation](https://react.dev/)\n- [TypeScript Handbook](https://www.typescriptlang.org/docs/)\n- [TanStack Query](https://tanstack.com/query/latest)\n- [Zustand](https://zustand-demo.pmnd.rs/)\n- [Vitest](https://vitest.dev/)\n- [Testing Library](https://testing-library.com/)\n"
